CREATE TABLE user (
	id CHAR(32) NOT NULL, 
	email VARCHAR, 
	auth_provider VARCHAR NOT NULL, 
	oauth_id VARCHAR, 
	name VARCHAR NOT NULL, 
	department VARCHAR, 
	gender VARCHAR, 
	avatar_url VARCHAR, 
	dominant_hand VARCHAR, 
	rubber_forehand VARCHAR, 
	rubber_backhand VARCHAR, 
	global_mmr FLOAT NOT NULL, 
	role VARCHAR NOT NULL, 
	is_active BOOLEAN NOT NULL, 
	PRIMARY KEY (id)
)

CREATE TABLE seasonrecord (
	id CHAR(32) NOT NULL, 
	user_id CHAR(32) NOT NULL, 
	season_id VARCHAR NOT NULL, 
	season_lp FLOAT NOT NULL, 
	matches_played INTEGER NOT NULL, 
	wins INTEGER NOT NULL, 
	previous_rank INTEGER, 
	PRIMARY KEY (id), 
	FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES user (id), 
	FOREIGN KEY(season_id) REFERENCES season (id)
)

CREATE TABLE "match" (
	id CHAR(32) NOT NULL, 
	match_type VARCHAR NOT NULL, 
	format VARCHAR NOT NULL, 
	team_a_p1_id CHAR(32) NOT NULL, 
	team_a_p2_id CHAR(32), 
	team_b_p1_id CHAR(32) NOT NULL, 
	team_b_p2_id CHAR(32), 
	score_a INTEGER NOT NULL, 
	score_b INTEGER NOT NULL, 
	mmr_exchanged FLOAT NOT NULL, 
	lp_exchanged FLOAT NOT NULL, 
	status VARCHAR NOT NULL, 
	reported_by CHAR(32) NOT NULL, 
	season_id VARCHAR NOT NULL, 
	created_at DATETIME NOT NULL, 
	PRIMARY KEY (id), 
	FOREIGN KEY(team_a_p1_id) REFERENCES user (id), 
	FOREIGN KEY(team_a_p2_id) REFERENCES user (id), 
	FOREIGN KEY(team_b_p1_id) REFERENCES user (id), 
	FOREIGN KEY(team_b_p2_id) REFERENCES user (id), 
	FOREIGN KEY(reported_by) REFERENCES user (id), 
	FOREIGN KEY(season_id) REFERENCES season (id)
)
